Guava Margaritas
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/guava-margaritas/
Taste of Home Editorial Team
Thu, 18 Sep 2025 18:56:25 +0000

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2184585
While visiting family, I tasted a guava margarita and fell in love with the tropical flavors. I rushed home to create my own version! —Renee Page, Rochelle, Illinois
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>Ice cubes</li><li>2 cups guava nectar</li><li>1-1/2 cups tequila</li><li>1 cup fresh lime juice</li><li>1/2 cup simple syrup</li><li>1/4 cup triple sec</li><li>Lime wedges</li><li>Coarse sugar</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Guava Margaritas%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/guava-margaritas/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0AIce cubes%20%0A2 cups guava nectar%20%0A1-1/2 cups tequila%20%0A1 cup fresh lime juice%20%0A1/2 cup simple syrup%20%0A1/4 cup triple sec%20%0ALime wedges%20%0ACoarse sugar%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="19" height="19" viewBox="0 0 19 19" fill="none">
<g clip-path="url(#clip0_1070_10606)">
<path d="M13.0625 0.499023H5.1875C4.25586 0.499023 3.5 1.25488 3.5 2.18652V16.8115C3.5 17.7432 4.25586 18.499 5.1875 18.499H13.0625C13.9941 18.499 14.75 17.7432 14.75 16.8115V2.18652C14.75 1.25488 13.9941 0.499023 13.0625 0.499023ZM9.125 17.374C8.50273 17.374 8 16.8713 8 16.249C8 15.6268 8.50273 15.124 9.125 15.124C9.74727 15.124 10.25 15.6268 10.25 16.249C10.25 16.8713 9.74727 17.374 9.125 17.374ZM13.0625 13.5771C13.0625 13.8092 12.8727 13.999 12.6406 13.999H5.60938C5.37734 13.999 5.1875 13.8092 5.1875 13.5771V2.6084C5.1875 2.37637 5.37734 2.18652 5.60938 2.18652H12.6406C12.8727 2.18652 13.0625 2.37637 13.0625 2.6084V13.5771Z" fill="#005278"/>

<div class="recipe-ingredients-ad-wrapper">
</div>
</div>
<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>In a pitcher filled with ice cubes, combine guava nectar, tequila, lime juice, simple syrup and triple sec. Stir until condensation forms on outside of the pitcher, 15-20 seconds.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Moisten rims of 8 margarita or cocktail glasses with lime wedges. Sprinkle sugar on a plate; dip rims in sugar. Immediately serve over ice in prepared glasses (use a spoon while pouring to hold ice cubes in pitcher).</span></li></ol></div>
<div class="recipe-nutrition-facts">
<h2 class="recipe-nutrition-facts__heading">Nutrition Facts</h2>
<p>1 serving: 220 calories, 0 fat (0 saturated fat), 0 cholesterol, 15mg sodium, 28g carbohydrate (24g sugars, 1g fiber), 0 protein.</p>
</div>
Muffaletta Dip
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/muffaletta-dip/
Taste of Home Editorial Team
Thu, 18 Sep 2025 18:50:43 +0000

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2184583
I love everything about a Muffaletta sandwich, so I just had to make it into a dip. It makes for a great party appetizer! —Courtney Stultz, Weir, Kansas
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>8 ounces cream cheese, softened</li><li>2 teaspoons olive oil</li><li>1 teaspoon minced garlic</li><li>1 teaspoon red wine vinegar</li><li>1 teaspoon minced fresh parsley</li><li>1/2 cup chopped pitted green olives</li><li>1/4 cup chopped pitted Kalamata or Greek olives</li><li>1/4 cup chopped ripe olives</li><li>1/4 cup chopped roasted sweet red peppers</li><li>1/4 cup chopped pepperoncini</li><li>1 teaspoon capers, drained</li><li>Assorted crackers</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Muffaletta Dip%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/muffaletta-dip/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A8 ounces cream cheese, softened%20%0A2 teaspoons olive oil%20%0A1 teaspoon minced garlic%20%0A1 teaspoon red wine vinegar%20%0A1 teaspoon minced fresh parsley%20%0A1/2 cup chopped pitted green olives%20%0A1/4 cup chopped pitted Kalamata or Greek olives%20%0A1/4 cup chopped ripe olives%20%0A1/4 cup chopped roasted sweet red peppers%20%0A1/4 cup chopped pepperoncini%20%0A1 teaspoon capers, drained%20%0AAssorted crackers%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">

<div class="recipe-ingredients-ad-wrapper">

</div>
<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>In a small bowl, beat cream cheese, olive oil, garlic, red wine vinegar and parsley until well combined. Fold in olives, peppers, pepperoncini and capers. Serve with assorted crackers.</span></li></ol></div>
<div class="recipe-nutrition-facts">
<h2 class="recipe-nutrition-facts__heading">Nutrition Facts</h2>
<p>1/4 cup: 146 calories, 14g fat (6g saturated fat), 29mg cholesterol, 401mg sodium, 4g carbohydrate (1g sugars, 0 fiber), 2g protein.</p>

Orange Snow Balls
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/orange-snow-balls/
Taste of Home Editorial Team
Thu, 18 Sep 2025 18:46:09 +0000

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2184581
These snow balls are perfectly sweet with just a hint of tart orange flavor. Everyone loves them, and I always get recipe requests when I bring them to a party. —Brooke Wofford, Travelers Rest, South Carolina
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>1 package (11 ounces) vanilla wafers</li><li>2/3 cup chopped pecans</li><li>1/2 cup butter, melted</li><li>1/4 cup frozen orange juice concentrate, thawed</li><li>3 cups confectioners' sugar, divided</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Orange Snow Balls%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/orange-snow-balls/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A1 package (11 ounces) vanilla wafers%20%0A2/3 cup chopped pecans%20%0A1/2 cup butter, melted%20%0A1/4 cup frozen orange juice concentrate, thawed%20%0A3 cups confectioners' sugar, divided%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="19" height="19" viewBox="0 0 19 19" fill="none">
<g clip-path="url(#clip0_1070_10606)">
<path d="M13.0625 0.499023H5.1875C4.25586 0.499023 3.5 1.25488 3.5 2.18652V16.8115C3.5 17.7432 4.25586 18.499 5.1875 18.499H13.0625C13.9941 18.499 14.75 17.7432 14.75 16.8115V2.18652C14.75 1.25488 13.9941 0.499023 13.0625 0.499023ZM9.125 17.374C8.50273 17.374 8 16.8713 8 16.249C8 15.6268 8.50273 15.124 9.125 15.124C9.74727 15.124 10.25 15.6268 10.25 16.249C10.25 16.8713 9.74727 17.374 9.125 17.374ZM13.0625 13.5771C13.0625 13.8092 12.8727 13.999 12.6406 13.999H5.60938C5.37734 13.999 5.1875 13.8092 5.1875 13.5771V2.6084C5.1875 2.37637 5.37734 2.18652 5.60938 2.18652H12.6406C12.8727 2.18652 13.0625 2.37637 13.0625 2.6084V13.5771Z" fill="#005278"/>
</g>

<clipPath id="clip0_1070_10606">
<rect width="18" height="18" fill="white" transform="translate(0.5 0.499023)"/>
</clipPath>
</defs>
</svg>
<span>Text Ingredients</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="recipe-ingredients-ad-wrapper">
</div>
</div>
<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>Place vanilla wafer cookies and pecans in a food processor; pulse until fine crumbs form. Add butter, thawed orange juice concentrate and one cup of confectioners sugar; pulse until mixture comes together.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Shape mixture into 1-in. balls; roll in remaining confectioners sugar. Store at room temperature.</span></li></ol></div>
<div class="recipe-nutrition-facts">
<h2 class="recipe-nutrition-facts__heading">Nutrition Facts</h2>
<p>1 piece: 112 calories, 6g fat (2g saturated fat), 9mg cholesterol, 60mg sodium, 13g carbohydrate (10g sugars, 0 fiber), 1g protein.</p>
</div>

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2184285
<p>We're calling it: The Stanley Cross Bottle is fall's best-kept accessory secret. </p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-cross-bottle/">The Stanley Cross Bottle Is Here—And We&#8217;re Obsessed With the Dazzling Midnight Glitz Hue</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>Last month, Stanley pulled a fast one and restocked the coveted <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-midnight-glitz/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-midnight-glitz/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Midnight Glitz ProTour tumblers</a> without warning. If you snagged one before they sold out, lucky you. (I managed to buy one, and yes, they&rsquo;re even more dazzling IRL.)</p><p>If you missed the restock and want a taste of the shimmering Midnight Glitz hue, it&rsquo;s still up for grabs in one sleek style: the <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-midnight-glitz-stanley-cross-bottle-23-oz-1" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-midnight-glitz-stanley-cross-bottle-23-oz-1" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Stanley Cross Bottle</a>. Here&rsquo;s everything you need to know about the bottle that&rsquo;s keeping the shimmer alive.</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Stanley-Midnight-Glitz-Cross-Bottle_via-stanley1913.com_GSedit.jpg?w=892" alt="Stanley Midnight Glitz Cross Bottle" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 1"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Stanley Midnight Glitz Cross Bottle</h3></div><div class="ap-card-description"><p>An on-the-go hydrator comes in one of our all-time favorite Stanley hues.</p></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop at Stanley" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-midnight-glitz-stanley-cross-bottle-23-oz-1" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop at Stanley" data-retailer-name="Stanley" data-product-name="Stanley Midnight Glitz Cross Bottle" data-product-retailer="Stanley" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop at Stanley</a></p></div></div></div><h2>What is the Stanley Cross Bottle?</h2><p>The <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-midnight-glitz-stanley-cross-bottle-23-oz-1" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-midnight-glitz-stanley-cross-bottle-23-oz-1" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">23-ounce Stanley Cross Bottle</a> is your go-anywhere, hydrate-anytime companion. With a tethered lid, leakproof design and comfy jacquard strap, it&rsquo;s built for hands-free carry. Bonus: the silicone base softens every set-down, so there are no clunks and spills.</p><p>The Midnight Glitz shimmers as you move&mdash;sort of like a disco ball. It&rsquo;s a deep, glossy black with rainbow glitter that catches the light, and it&rsquo;s&nbsp;topped with a sheer purple lid and straw for a sophisticated cup with just the right amount of glitz.</p><p>If the Midnight Glitz colorway isn&rsquo;t your style, the <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-stanley-cross-bottle-23-oz%3Fvariant%3D44560048423039" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-stanley-cross-bottle-23-oz%3Fvariant%3D44560048423039" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Cross Bottle</a> also comes in 10 other hues like Rose Quartz, Mist and Cream.</p><h2>Is it worth the hype?</h2><p>We won&rsquo;t lie, we&rsquo;re kind of obsessed with how sleek the Cross Bottle looks. It&rsquo;s easily one of the prettiest sling-style water bottles out there, and honestly, perfect for travel and outdoor adventures. (No more accidentally leaving your bottle behind in the terminal&mdash;this one stays strapped on.)</p><p>It&rsquo;s got all the classic Stanley perks too: a removable straw and double-wall vacuum insulation to keep drinks cold for hours.</p><p>Yes, the price is a little higher than the <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-quencher-tumbler-review/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-quencher-tumbler-review/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Stanley Quencher tumbler</a>, but reviewers say it&rsquo;s worth it for a hands-free, ultra-portable bottle made for city exploring, trail walking and everything in between. Bacon Cheeseburger Pizza
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/bacon-cheeseburger-pizza/
Kate McKiernan
Thu, 18 Sep 2025 14:57:04 +0000

http://origin-www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/bacon-cheeseburger-pizza/
For the nights you crave a burger and a slice at the same time, bacon cheeseburger pizza is your ticket to happiness.
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>1/2 pound ground beef</li><li>1 small onion, chopped</li><li>1 prebaked 12-inch pizza crust</li><li>1 can (8 ounces) pizza sauce</li><li>6 bacon strips, cooked and crumbled</li><li>20 dill pickle slices</li><li>2 cups shredded part-skim mozzarella cheese</li><li>2 cups shredded cheddar cheese</li><li>1 teaspoon pizza or Italian seasoning</li>		</ul>

Directions	</h2>

Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need to Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/aldi-sourdough-kit/
Hayley Schueneman
Wed, 17 Sep 2025 21:35:34 +0000
Grocery Stores
New Products
News
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2183811
<p>It's a loaf story, baby, just say bread.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/aldi-sourdough-kit/">Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need to Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>It&rsquo;s been a very busy year for Taylor Swift. She&rsquo;s fresh off of her record-breaking Eras Tour, she just regained ownership of all of her master recordings, and she recently <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-travis-kelce-engagement-party-menu/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-travis-kelce-engagement-party-menu/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">got engaged to Travis Kelce</a>. If this was a movie, well, the credits would be playing right now.</p><p>But if I&rsquo;ve learned anything from following Taylor Swift, it&rsquo;s that she never stops creating. In fact, her twelfth studio album, <em>The Life of a Showgirl</em>, drops in just two weeks. The studio isn&rsquo;t the only place where she gets in the creative mood though. On a recent episode of the <em>New Heights</em> podcast, Taylor revealed some of her favorite hobbies. Or, as she put it, &ldquo;I&rsquo;d say all my hobbies could be categorized as, like, hobbies you could have had in the 1700s.&rdquo;</p><p>We know <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-chai-cookies/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-chai-cookies/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Taylor likes baking cookies</a>, and it turns out that another of those hobbies is making sourdough bread. I need to know who feeds her starter when she&rsquo;s on tour! Details aside, I&rsquo;ve been trying to get motivated to get back into sourdough. The stars seem to have aligned, because Aldi just dropped a sourdough kit that has everything you need. Or should I say, <em>knead</em>.</p><h2>What&rsquo;s in Aldi&rsquo;s sourdough kit?</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2183885" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Aldi-Just-Dropped-Everything-You-Need-to-Make-Sourdough-Like-Taylor-Swift_Courtesy-Aldi.jpg?fit=700%2C1024" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need To Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift Courtesy Aldi" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Courtesy Aldi"></p><p>Making sourdough bread requires a few advanced techniques and special tools. Think of this Aldi sourdough kit as having everything but the sourdough starter. It includes:</p><ul><li><strong>Bench scraper:</strong> You&rsquo;ll need this to divide the dough and to shape the dough into a loaf while creating surface tension.</li><li><strong>Dough whisk:</strong> Different from <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/whisk-types-guide/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/whisk-types-guide/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">French whisks and flat whisks</a>, a dough whisk is made specifically for thicker batters and doughs.</li><li><strong>Lame with two blades:</strong> Bread lames are one of the <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/bread-baking-essentials/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/bread-baking-essentials/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">essential bread baking tools</a>. Use these to <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/bread-scoring/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/bread-scoring/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">score your loaves</a> with all sorts of designs (besides aesthetics, scoring bread lets steam escape for a more even bake).</li><li><strong>Proofing basket:</strong> Also called a banneton, this is a lined basket that helps keep the shape of your loaf while it proofs.</li></ul><p>The best part is that you get all of these materials for $14.99. It&rsquo;s an incredible value, especially since you can use these tools over and over again to make plenty of loaves.</p><h2>When is Aldi&rsquo;s sourdough kit available?</h2><p>This kit is available right now at Aldi stores nationwide, while supplies last. Since it&rsquo;s an Aldi Find, it lives by the store&rsquo;s &ldquo;here today, gone tomorrow&rdquo; credo. That means that once they&rsquo;re sold out, they&rsquo;re gone for good. So if you&rsquo;re ready to enter your sourdough era, then it&rsquo;s time to take a &ldquo;Getaway Car&rdquo; to Aldi!</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-favorite-candy/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-favorite-candy/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Tried Taylor Swift&rsquo;s Favorite Candy, and Now It&rsquo;s My Favorite Candy Too</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-pop-tarts-recipe/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-pop-tarts-recipe/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Made Taylor Swift&rsquo;s Viral Homemade Pop-Tarts&mdash;Here&rsquo;s What I Thought</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-super-bowl-party?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-super-bowl-party?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">11 Ideas for a Super Bowl Party (Taylor&rsquo;s Version)</a></li></ul><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/aldi-sourdough-kit/">Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need to Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>

Costco Wine Recall: Bottles of Prosecco Are at Risk of Shattering
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-wine-recall-september-2025/
Hayley Schueneman
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 22:56:32 +0000
News
Recalls
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2183830
<p>Check your wine rack and your fridge.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-wine-recall-september-2025/">Costco Wine Recall: Bottles of Prosecco Are at Risk of Shattering</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p data-start="195" data-end="502">If you picked up a bottle of Kirkland Signature Prosecco Valdobbiadene at Costco earlier this year, then you&rsquo;ll want to double-check your stash. Costco has issued a recall for certain bottles due to a safety issue that could cause them to break unexpectedly&mdash;even if they&rsquo;re just sitting unopened on your wine rack. Here&rsquo;s what you need to know.</p><h2>What caused the recall?</h2><p>According to a <a href="https://cdn.bfldr.com/U447IH35/as/3q6998t8pfg5hhjpkcpgvbc/FinalKSProseccoValdoMemberLetter" data-name="cdn.bfldr.com/U447IH35/as/3q6998t8pfg5hhjpkcpgvbc/FinalKSProseccoValdoMemberLetter" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">notice sent to Costco members</a>, some bottles of the Prosecco may spontaneously shatter&mdash;even if they haven&rsquo;t been touched. That&rsquo;s a serious safety risk, as flying glass could cause injury. Costco and Ethica Wines (the product&rsquo;s importer) are urging members to check their bottles and handle them with care.</p><h2>What stores sold the wine?</h2><p data-start="1014" data-end="1222">This recall only affects Kirkland Signature Prosecco Valdobbiadene, which is a Costco-exclusive brand. If you purchased Prosecco from Costco in any of the following states, it could be part of the recall: Iowa, Illinois, Indiana, Kentucky, Michigan, Minnesota, Missouri, North Dakota, Nebraska, Ohio, South Dakota and Wisconsin.</p><h2>How do I know if I have a recalled wine?</h2><p>Here&rsquo;s what to look for:</p><p><strong>Kirkland Signature Prosecco Valdobbiadene</strong></p><ul><li>Item number on the label: 1879870</li><li>Purchase date: Between April 25, 2025 and August 26, 2025</li><li>Costco location you purchased from was in one of the states listed above</li></ul><p>If all of those match, your wine bottle is affected.</p><h2>What should I do next?</h2><p data-start="1834" data-end="2031">Do not try to open the bottle, and do not bring it back into the store. To safely dispose of it, wrap it in paper towels, put it in a plastic bag, and place it in the trash. Then, bring the recall notice (or just your receipt) to your local Costco for a full refund.</p><p data-start="1834" data-end="2031">If you have questions, you can contact Ethica Wines at customercare@ethicawines.com or by calling 786-810-7132 Monday through Friday between 8 a.m. and 6 p.m. EST.</p><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-wine-recall-september-2025/">Costco Wine Recall: Bottles of Prosecco Are at Risk of Shattering</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
This Is Margot Robbie’s Go-To Breakfast Order
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbie-breakfast/
Hayley Schueneman
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 22:30:09 +0000
News
People in Food
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2155795
<p>She's a millennial through and through!</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbie-breakfast/">This Is Margot Robbie&#8217;s Go-To Breakfast Order</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>Margot Robbie is without a doubt one of the biggest stars of the moment. I&rsquo;ve been a huge fan of her work since her role as Tonya Harding in <em>I, Tonya</em>. She and <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ryan-gosling-favorite-dessert/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ryan-gosling-favorite-dessert/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ryan Gosling</a>&nbsp;were absolutely iconic together in <em>Barbie</em>. Soon, we&rsquo;ll see Margot as Catherine in the upcoming adaptation of <em>Wuthering Heights</em>. And just this week, the newest film in her portfolio, <em>A Big Bold Beautiful Journey</em>, premiered.</p><p>When she&rsquo;s not on set, she&rsquo;s most likely working on her alcohol brand, <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbies-favorite-cocktail/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbies-favorite-cocktail/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Papa Salt</a>. It&rsquo;s an Australian-based, award-winning gin company that she launched with her husband and friends.</p><p>I wondered what she eats to keep up her energy for such a busy calendar. And honestly, as a fellow millennial, I am not surprised!</p><h2>What does Margot Robbie eat for breakfast?</h2><p>It turns out that she has a very specific <a href="https://www.vogue.com/article/margot-robbie-barbie-summer-cover-2023-interview" data-name="www.vogue.com/article/margot-robbie-barbie-summer-cover-2023-interview" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">avocado toast order</a>. Rather than smashing a few pieces of avocado on toast and calling it a day, she turns hers into a veritable feast by adding grilled halloumi and Australian bacon (a leaner, less fatty cut than American-style bacon). I love the idea of dressing up a basic combo like avocado and bread with a protein!</p><p>And when she isn&rsquo;t ordering avocado toast, she is having porridge with blackberries and a smoothie. She <a href="https://www.purewow.com/food/margot-robbie-red-carpet-ready-smoothie-recipe" data-name="www.purewow.com/food/margot-robbie-red-carpet-ready-smoothie-recipe" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">has said in interviews</a> that she particularly likes green smoothies (like <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-made-the-green-smoothie-reese-witherspoon-drinks-every-day/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-made-the-green-smoothie-reese-witherspoon-drinks-every-day/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Reese Witherspoon</a>), and her favorite recipe includes kale, apple and banana. What I love most about Margot Robbie&rsquo;s go-to breakfast is that it&rsquo;s something relatable that I could whip up right now.</p><p>Oatmeal and porridge is certainly a popular celeb breakfast, considering that people like<a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-does-kate-middleton-eat-for-breakfast/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-does-kate-middleton-eat-for-breakfast/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links"> Kate Middleton</a>, <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-breakfast-2025/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-breakfast-2025/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ina Garten</a> and <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/willie-nelson-breakfast/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/willie-nelson-breakfast/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Willie Nelson</a> all enjoy it in the morning!</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a Tyler Smith’s French Onion Sliders
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/tyler-smith-french-onion-sliders/
Tyler Smith
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 22:28:49 +0000
Burgers
Creator
Dishes & Beverages
Recipes
Sandwiches & Wraps
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2183937
These French onion cheeseburger sliders are the ultimate bite-sized indulgence. Juicy beef patties are topped with caramelized onions and melted cheese, all tucked into soft slider buns for a savory, melty twist on a classic. Perfect for game day parties or anytime you’re craving big flavor in a small package. —Tyler Smith, Virginia Beach, Virginia
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>3/4 cup butter, divided</li><li>1 large sweet onion, thinly sliced</li><li>1 large red onion, thinly sliced</li><li>2 tablespoons Worcestershire sauce, divided</li><li>2 pounds ground sirloin</li><li>1 envelope onion soup mix</li><li>1 tablespoon salt</li><li>1/2 tablespoon pepper</li><li>1 package Hawaiian sweet rolls (24 count)</li><li>12 slices Swiss cheese</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>GARLIC HORSERADISH AIOLI:</b></li><li>6 garlic cloves, roasted</li><li>1/2 cup mayonnaise</li><li>1/4 cup sour cream</li><li>1/2 medium lemon, juiced</li><li>2 tablespoons minced chives</li><li>1 tablespoon prepared horseradish</li><li>1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Tyler Smith’s French Onion Sliders%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/tyler-smith-french-onion-sliders/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A3/4 cup butter, divided%20%0A1 large sweet onion, thinly sliced%20%0A1 large red onion, thinly sliced%20%0A2 tablespoons Worcestershire sauce, divided%20%0A2 pounds ground sirloin%20%0A1 envelope onion soup mix%20%0A1 tablespoon salt%20%0A1/2 tablespoon pepper%20%0A1 package Hawaiian sweet rolls (24 count)%20%0A12 slices Swiss cheese%20%0AGARLIC HORSERADISH AIOLI:%20%0A6 garlic cloves, roasted%20%0A1/2 cup mayonnaise%20%0A1/4 cup sour cream%20%0A1/2 medium lemon, juiced%20%0A2 tablespoons minced chives%20%0A1 tablespoon prepared horseradish%20%0A1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>Preheat oven to 400°. Heat 1/2 cup butter in a large skillet over medium heat. Add onions; cook 5-6 minutes or until starting to lightly brown. Reduce heat to medium-low. Cook 25 minutes, stirring every 5 minutes. Add 1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce, and stir to combine. Continue cooking until onions are a deep brown color and very soft, 15-20 minutes longer.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Meanwhile, in a large bowl, combine beef, soup mix, remaining 1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce, salt and pepper; mix lightly but thoroughly. On a foil-lined baking sheet, shape beef mixture into a rectangle slightly larger than the size of the Hawaiian rolls (about 9x13-in.). Bake until a thermometer reads 160°, 15-20 minutes. Set aside.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a medium bowl, mash garlic with a fork until smooth. Add remaining aioli ingredients until well combined. Refrigerate until ready to use.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Reduce oven temperature to 350°. Without separating rolls, cut rolls in half horizontally; arrange bottom halves onto a parchment-lined baking sheet. Layer bottom halves with beef, caramelized onions and Swiss cheese; replace top halves of rolls. Melt remaining 1/4 cup butter; brush over rolls.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Bake until cheese is melted and buns are browned, 10-15 minutes. Garnish with additional minced fresh chives, if desired; serve with prepared aioli.</span></li></ol></div>
Tam To’s One-Pot Tomato Salmon
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/tam-to-one-pot-tomato-salmon/
Tam To
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 22:01:16 +0000
Creator
Fish & Seafood
Ingredients
Recipes
Salmon
Salmon Fillet
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2183930
This one-pot tomato salmon recipe is a fresh spin on the classic Vietnamese dish of stuffed tofu in tomato sauce. The salmon is seared and cooked to tender perfection in a bright tomato sauce that's bursting with umami flavor from fish sauce. Serve it over rice or pasta, or enjoy it on its own. —Tam To, Los Angeles, California
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>1-1/2 cups cherry tomatoes</li><li>1 shallot, halved</li><li>3 garlic cloves</li><li>2 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil, divided</li><li>1 tablespoon fish sauce</li><li>1 tablespoon tomato paste</li><li>2 salmon fillets</li><li> Salt and pepper to taste</li><li>2 plum tomatoes, quartered</li><li>Thinly sliced green onions, for garnish</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Tam To’s One-Pot Tomato Salmon%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/tam-to-one-pot-tomato-salmon/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A1-1/2 cups cherry tomatoes%20%0A1 shallot, halved%20%0A3 garlic cloves%20%0A2 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil, divided%20%0A1 tablespoon fish sauce%20%0A1 tablespoon tomato paste%20%0A2 salmon fillets%20%0A Salt and pepper to taste%20%0A2 plum tomatoes, quartered%20%0AThinly sliced green onions, for garnish%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>In a food processor or blender, combine cherry tomatoes, shallot, garlic, 1 tablespoon oil, fish sauce and tomato paste until finely chopped. Set aside.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a large nonstick skillet, heat remaining tablespoon oil over medium heat. Season salmon with salt and pepper. Sear salmon on each side until golden brown, 2-3 minutes a side. </span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Pour reserved tomato sauce around salmon. Arrange plum tomatoes in sauce. Cook, covered, 2-3 minutes. Uncover and cook 2-3 minutes longer. If desired, garnish with green onions before serving.</span></li></ol></div>
Alex Bala’s Buffalo Chicken Egg Rolls
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/alex-bala-buffalo-chicken-egg-rolls/
Alex Bala
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 19:44:26 +0000
Air Fryer
Appliances
Creator
Dishes & Beverages
Egg Rolls
Gear
Recipes
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2183899
Buffalo chicken egg rolls are the perfect mashup of comfort food and party snack. They're golden on the outside and creamy and spicy on the inside, and the first thing to go at the party! —Alex Bala, Longmont, Colorado
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>2 rotisserie chicken breasts, shredded</li><li>2 teaspoons onion powder, divided</li><li>2 teaspoons garlic powder, divided</li><li>1 pinch kosher salt</li><li>5 tablespoons unsalted butter</li><li>1/4 cup diced sweet red pepper</li><li>1/4 cup diced green pepper</li><li>1/2 medium red onion, diced</li><li>2 tablespoons diced jalapeno peppers</li><li>1 teaspoon ground cumin</li><li>1 teaspoon chili powder</li><li>1 teaspoon smoked paprika</li><li>1 package (8 ounces) cream cheese, softened</li><li>1/4 cup hot sauce</li><li>12 egg roll wrappers</li><li>2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese</li><li>1/4 cup neutral oil, for brushing</li><li>Optional: Ranch or blue cheese dressing</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Alex Bala’s Buffalo Chicken Egg Rolls%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/alex-bala-buffalo-chicken-egg-rolls/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A2 rotisserie chicken breasts, shredded%20%0A2 teaspoons onion powder, divided%20%0A2 teaspoons garlic powder, divided%20%0A1 pinch kosher salt%20%0A5 tablespoons unsalted butter%20%0A1/4 cup diced sweet red pepper%20%0A1/4 cup diced green pepper%20%0A1/2 medium red onion, diced%20%0A2 tablespoons diced jalapeno peppers%20%0A1 teaspoon ground cumin%20%0A1 teaspoon chili powder%20%0A1 teaspoon smoked paprika%20%0A1 package (8 ounces) cream cheese, softened%20%0A1/4 cup hot sauce%20%0A12 egg roll wrappers%20%0A2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese%20%0A1/4 cup neutral oil, for brushing%20%0AOptional: Ranch or blue cheese dressing%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>In a large bowl, toss shredded chicken with 1 teaspoon garlic powder, 1 teaspoon onion powder and salt until well combined; set aside.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a medium saucepan, melt butter over medium heat. Add peppers, onion and jalapenos. Cook until tender. Add remaining 1 teaspoon onion powder, 1 teaspoon garlic powder, cumin, chili powder and smoked paprika. Stir in cream cheese and hot sauce; cook until smooth and bubbly.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Pour sauce over shredded chicken, toss to coat. Cool slightly.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Position an egg roll wrapper with one point toward you. Place a spoonful of chicken mixture in the center. Top with a sprinkle of mozzarella cheese. Fold bottom corner over filling; fold sides toward center over filling. Roll toward the remaining point. Moisten top corner with water; press to seal. Repeat with remaining wrappers and filling.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Preheat air fryer to 400°. Brush rolls lightly with oil. Place rolls in a single layer in air-fryer basket. Cook until brown and crisp, flipping halfway though, about 10 minutes.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Serve warm with ranch or blue cheese dressing, if desired.</span></li></ol></div>
Pumpkin Truffles
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/pumpkin-truffles/
Susan Bronson
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 21:23:04 +0000

White Chocolate
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2182268
These bite-sized pumpkin truffles look and taste like pumpkins, thanks to pumpkin butter and puree mixed into the white chocolate and graham cracker base.
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>4 ounces white baking chocolate, broken into pieces</li><li>3 ounces cream cheese, softened</li><li>1/3 cup canned pumpkin</li><li>2 tablespoons pumpkin butter</li><li>1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice</li><li>1-1/2 cups graham cracker crumbs</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>SUGAR COATING AND GARNISH:</b></li><li>2 tablespoons sugar</li><li>1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice</li><li>Miniature semisweet chocolate chips, for garnish</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Pumpkin Truffles%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/pumpkin-truffles/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A4 ounces white baking chocolate, broken into pieces%20%0A3 ounces cream cheese, softened%20%0A1/3 cup canned pumpkin%20%0A2 tablespoons pumpkin butter%20%0A1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice%20%0A1-1/2 cups graham cracker crumbs%20%0ASUGAR COATING AND GARNISH:%20%0A2 tablespoons sugar%20%0A1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice%20%0AMiniature semisweet chocolate chips, for garnish%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="19" height="19" viewBox="0 0 19 19" fill="none">
<g clip-path="url(#clip0_1070_10606)">
<path d="M13.0625 0.499023H5.1875C4.25586 0.499023 3.5 1.25488 3.5 2.18652V16.8115C3.5 17.7432 4.25586 18.499 5.1875 18.499H13.0625C13.9941 18.499 14.75 17.7432 14.75 16.8115V2.18652C14.75 1.25488 13.9941 0.499023 13.0625 0.499023ZM9.125 17.374C8.50273 17.374 8 16.8713 8 16.249C8 15.6268 8.50273 15.124 9.125 15.124C9.74727 15.124 10.25 15.6268 10.25 16.249C10.25 16.8713 9.74727 17.374 9.125 17.374ZM13.0625 13.5771C13.0625 13.8092 12.8727 13.999 12.6406 13.999H5.60938C5.37734 13.999 5.1875 13.8092 5.1875 13.5771V2.6084C5.1875 2.37637 5.37734 2.18652 5.60938 2.18652H12.6406C12.8727 2.18652 13.0625 2.37637 13.0625 2.6084V13.5771Z" fill="#005278"/>

<span>Text Ingredients</span>

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>Place white chocolate pieces in a microwave-safe bowl. Cook at 50% power for 90 seconds; stir. Microwave at 30-second intervals until melted, stirring between intervals. Set aside for 5 minutes to cool.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a large bowl, beat cream cheese and pumpkin puree until smooth. Stir in pumpkin butter, melted white chocolate and pumpkin pie spice. Add graham cracker crumbs; stir until well-combined and a thick dough forms. Cover and refrigerate until dough is firm, at least 2 hours or overnight.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
To make coating, in a small bowl, mix together sugar and pumpkin pie spice; set aside.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Scoop chilled dough into tablespoonfuls; roll into balls. Roll in the sugar-spice mixture until evenly coated. Roll a toothpick or blunt edge of a knife gently into the sides to make the pumpkin's ridges. Top each with a mini chocolate chip to make the stem.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Store in an airtight container in the refrigerator until ready to serve.</span></li></ol></div>

A dirty chai espresso martini is where cozy fall flavor meets speakeasy glamour.

<li>1 cup sugar</li><li>1 cup water</li><li>2 Chai tea bags</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>MARTINI:</b></li><li>Ice cubes</li><li>2 ounces chilled brewed espresso or cold brew concentrate</li><li>1-1/2 ounces vodka</li><li>1/2 ounce Chai tea simple syrup</li><li>1/2 ounce coffee liqueur</li><li>Coffee beans or star anise pod, for garnish</li>		</ul>

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span><span data-teams="true">To make the syrup, in a small saucepan over medium-high heat, add sugar and water. Bring to a boil. Cook until sugar is dissolved, 4-5 minutes, stirring frequently. Reduce heat, add tea bags and simmer until fragrant, another 4-5 minutes.</span> Remove from heat; discard tea bags. Let cool.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
To make the martini, chill a martini glass. Fill a shaker halfway with ice cubes. Add espresso, vodka, chai syrup and coffee liqueur. Place shaker lid on top; shake 20 seconds or until the shaker is frosty and contents are frothy. Strain into chilled martini glass. Garnish with coffee beans or star anise. Serve immediately.</span></li></ol></div>
<div class="recipe-nutrition-facts">
<h2 class="recipe-nutrition-facts__heading">Nutrition Facts</h2>
<p>1 martini: 220 calories, 0 fat (0 saturated fat), 0 cholesterol, 10mg sodium, 25g carbohydrate (22g sugars, 0 fiber), 0 protein.</p>

I Tried the New Popeyes x Hot Ones Menu—Here’s How Spicy It Really Is
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-hot-ones-menu/
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-hot-ones-menu/#respond
Joseph Erbentraut
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 14:58:49 +0000
New Products
News
Restaurants
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2183556
<p>The fast-food chain's new collab lets you pretend you're a celebrity across the table from Sean Evans. </p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-hot-ones-menu/">I Tried the New Popeyes x Hot Ones Menu—Here&#8217;s How Spicy It Really Is</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>There is no pop culture phenomenon quite like Hot Ones. Ten years ago, the YouTube talk show launched, and host Sean Evans has been alarming celebrities with probing questions and burning-hot wings ever since. In that decade, the show has amassed a cult following of more than 15 million subscribers and endless merch and internet memes.</p><p>It was really only a matter of time before a fast-food chain linked up with Hot Ones, and that&rsquo;s exactly what <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-ghost-pepper-chicken-sandwich-review/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-ghost-pepper-chicken-sandwich-review/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">Popeyes</a> has done with its new Popeyes x Hot Ones menu. The menu is now available for a limited time, and I bravely tried everything.</p><h2><strong>What&rsquo;s on the new Popeyes x Hot Ones menu?</strong></h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2183572" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Tried-the-New-Popeyes-x-Hot-Ones-Menu_popeyes-hot-ones-2_Joe-Erbentraut-for-taste-of-home.jpg?fit=700%2C1024" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Tried The New Popeyes X Hot Ones Menu Popeyes Hot Ones 2 Joe Erbentraut For Taste Of Home" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="JOE ERBENTRAUT FOR TASTE OF HOME"></p><p>The new menu has four items. As a nod to the hit YouTube series, the offerings are available in ascending order of spice level:</p><ul><li><strong>Sizzlin&rsquo; Sriracha Dippers:</strong> These Chicken Dippers are said to be mild. They are marinated in pickled garlic Sriracha and served with a Last Dab Ranch dip cup and a fiery Sriracha sachet.</li><li><strong>Smokin&rsquo; Rojo Sandwich:</strong> This is the chain&rsquo;s iconic <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/we-went-to-8-restaurants-to-find-the-best-fast-food-chicken-sandwich/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/we-went-to-8-restaurants-to-find-the-best-fast-food-chicken-sandwich/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">fried chicken sandwich</a> topped with a medium-spicy Hot Ones Los Calientes Rojo spread, complete with the chain&rsquo;s signature brioche bun and tangy pickle slices.</li><li><strong>Darin&rsquo; Dab Ghost Wings:</strong> Popeyes&rsquo; <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-chicken-wing-restaurants/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-chicken-wing-restaurants/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">classic chicken wings</a> (available either bone-in or boneless) are dusted with a &ldquo;very hot&rdquo; ghost pepper dry rub. The wings are served with a Last Dab Ranch dip cup.</li><li><strong>The Last Dab:</strong> Iconic to the Hot Ones brand, the Last Dab sauce sachet (different from the ranch cup) lets serious heat seekers add a final &ldquo;extremely hot&rdquo; dab to their wings.</li></ul><h2><strong>Is the Popeyes Hot Ones menu actually spicy?</strong></h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2183571" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Tried-the-New-Popeyes-x-Hot-Ones-Menu_popeyes-hot-ones-1_Joe-Erbentraut-for-taste-of-home.jpg?fit=700%2C1024" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Tried The New Popeyes X Hot Ones Menu Popeyes Hot Ones 1 Joe Erbentraut For Taste Of Home" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="JOE ERBENTRAUT FOR TASTE OF HOME"></p><p>Far too often in recent years, fast-food chains have launched limited-edition spicy menu items that fail to bring the heat. I&rsquo;m happy to report that this was not the case here.</p><p>To stay true to the Hot Ones ethos, I began my tasting of the Popeyes Hot Ones menu with the most mild item: the Sizzlin&rsquo; Sriracha Dippers. I did not receive Sriracha with my order, sadly, so I dipped the chicken instead into the Last Dab Ranch dip. This dip caught me off guard&mdash;it was tangy and creamy as any good ranch should be, but it packed a bounty of heat that lingered on my tongue. Still, as spicy as it was, it was not heat just for heat&rsquo;s sake&mdash;it kept bringing me back for more.</p><p>Next, I tried the Smokin&rsquo; Rojo Sandwich, which was a bit of a letdown. After experiencing the spicy ranch dip, the heat coming from the Los Calientes Rojo spread felt much more mild and was overwhelmingly smoky, a flavor profile I don&rsquo;t personally enjoy. Still, the chain&rsquo;s chicken sandwich is beloved for a reason, so I can&rsquo;t complain too much!</p><p>Then, it was time for the Darin&rsquo; Dab Ghost Wings. The heat on the wings themselves comes from the dry rub. Most of the dry rub on my order had been knocked off the breading and sank to the bottom of the box, so I found the wings to be surprisingly tolerable.</p><p>Finally, it was time for the ultimate test: The Last Dab sauce. I fully went for it, feeling brave after two &ldquo;rounds&rdquo; that were less spicy than I had expected. I chose the wing with the most visible dry rub and squirted a large dose of the dab sauce on top.</p><p>At first, I was underwhelmed&mdash;and then the heat crept up on me, and I wished that my mouth could exit my body for a couple of minutes while my eyes watered and my throat tickled. Indeed, The Last Dab lived up to its hype.</p><p>All things considered, I was impressed by the Popeyes x Hot Ones menu and grateful that nobody was asking me questions while a camera captured my every move. The Last Dab Ranch is one heck of a dip, and The Last Dab hot sauce is, indeed, not for the weak.</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-tried-the-new-mcdonalds-gold-sauce-and-it-tastes-like-sweet-smoky-heaven/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-tried-the-new-mcdonalds-gold-sauce-and-it-tastes-like-sweet-smoky-heaven/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Tried the New McDonald&rsquo;s Gold Sauce and It Tastes Like Sweet, Smoky Heaven</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-easy-appetizer/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-easy-appetizer/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ina Garten Just Shared Her Easiest Appetizer Recipe Ever</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-genius-gourmet-sparkling-protein-drink-review/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-genius-gourmet-sparkling-protein-drink-review/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">A New Protein Drink Has Entered the Market, and You&rsquo;ll Never Guess What It Is</a></li></ul><script async type="text/javascript" src="//tracking.skyword.com/tracker.js?contentId=281474980466560"></script><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-hot-ones-menu/">I Tried the New Popeyes x Hot Ones Menu—Here&#8217;s How Spicy It Really Is</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>

Cheers to the Best Cheap Champagne (Under $20 a Pop!)

Lisa A. Kaminski
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 00:48:48 +0000
Beverages
Dishes & Beverages

Stuff We Love
Stuff We Love Kitchen
Taste Tests
Test Kitchen

http://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=collection&p=830391
<p>Looking for bubbly on a budget? Our Test Kitchen sampled 20 different bottles to find the best cheap champagne for your celebrations.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/the-best-cheap-champagne/">Cheers to the Best Cheap Champagne (Under $20 a Pop!)</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>

That&rsquo;s precisely what you get when you <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-open-a-champagne-bottle-the-right-way/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-open-a-champagne-bottle-the-right-way/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">pop open</a> a bottle of&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fbuywinesonline.com%2Fproducts%2Fcupcake-vineyards-prosecco-750-ml" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fbuywinesonline.com%2Fproducts%2Fcupcake-vineyards-prosecco-750-ml" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Cupcake Prosecco</a>.</p><p>&ldquo;This one is light, bright and crisp,&rdquo; says <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/author/shannon-norris/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/author/shannon-norris/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Shannon Norris</a> in the Test Kitchen. Testers picked up notes of peach and melon in this bottle. Despite the name and the fruity subtleties, Cupcake Prosecco isn&rsquo;t overly sweet. Shannon explains that this bottle of bubbly walks a fine line between dry or sweet.</p><p>This bottle, which retails for about $10, is a great people-pleasing option to include at your <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/how-to-set-a-table-for-thanksgiving/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/how-to-set-a-table-for-thanksgiving/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">holiday table</a>.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 2"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Cook's California Champagne Brut</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$7.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-2"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Available for $7.99" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fcooks-california-champagne-brut%2Fp%2F1478750" champagne or a bottle of the pricey stuff, to be on the slightly dry side, reach for&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fcooks-california-champagne-brut%2Fp%2F1478750" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fcooks-california-champagne-brut%2Fp%2F1478750" like a special occasion. This pale California sparkling wine is packed with lots of large bubbles.</p><p>Shannon shares that a sip of this cheap champagne is &ldquo;light, crisp and full of bubbles.&rdquo; It has notes of tart green apple and lemon zest. &ldquo;This is one I&rsquo;d drink, serve and cook with in my kitchen,&rdquo; says Shannon.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Rondel-Brut-Cava_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=892" alt="Rondel Brut Cava Via Totalwine.com" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 3"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Rondel Brut Cava</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$11.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fcava%2Fbrut%2Frondel-brut-cava%2Fp%2F60170750" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="Rondel Brut Cava" data-product-price="11.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">11.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>Next time you&rsquo;re craving bubbles, our Test Kitchen recommends trying Cava, particularly&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fcava%2Fbrut%2Frondel-brut-cava%2Fp%2F60170750" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fcava%2Fbrut%2Frondel-brut-cava%2Fp%2F60170750" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Rondel Brut Cava</a>. This Spanish sparkling wine isn&rsquo;t as popular as Champagne or Prosecco, but it&rsquo;s absolutely fizzy and fantastic.</p><p>In fact, the bubbles in this bottle are what really stood out to our Test Kitchen team. Rondel&rsquo;s Cava was full of various-sized bubbles and held onto this fizz for a long time after pouring&mdash;three hours! That&rsquo;s pretty impressive says our Test Kitchen&rsquo;s <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/author/catherine-ward/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/author/catherine-ward/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Catherine Ward</a>, a lover of all things champagne. And remember, if you can&rsquo;t finish the bottle, you can <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-long-does-champagne-last-after-opening/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-long-does-champagne-last-after-opening/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">store opened champagne</a> for up to three days.</p><p>Beyond these bubbles, this Cava is wonderfully dry with flavors of pear and apple. These features make it a great complement to fish dishes and a striking yet welcome contrast to rich dinners. Give it a try with your <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-give-a-thanksgiving-toast/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-give-a-thanksgiving-toast/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Thanksgiving toast</a>! Keep a bottle of <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-non-alcoholic-champagnes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-non-alcoholic-champagnes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">non-alcoholic champagne</a> on hand for guests that prefer their drinks NA.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/19-Crimes-Snoop-Cali-Gold-Sparkling-Wine_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=892" alt="19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 4"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$12.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2F19-crimes-cali-gold-sparking-by-snoop-dogg%2Fp%2F346655750" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine" data-product-price="12.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">12.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>Snoop Dogg may have been pouring Chandon in his 2004 hit &ldquo;Drop It Like It&rsquo;s Hot,&rdquo; but these days he&rsquo;s popping open bottles of his own&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2F19-crimes-cali-gold-sparking-by-snoop-dogg%2Fp%2F346655750" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2F19-crimes-cali-gold-sparking-by-snoop-dogg%2Fp%2F346655750" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine</a>.</p><p>This California-made sparkler is pale in color with the <em>slightest</em> hint of green and &ldquo;refreshingly sweet,&rdquo; according to Shannon. It has a bold flavor for a sparkling wine with notes of lemon, nectarines and green apple for a crisp finish.</p><p>Made with a blend of Muscat and Riesling grapes (among others), this sweetness is no surprise. But it&rsquo;s a welcome flavor to pair with one of Snoop&rsquo;s favorite hobbies: baking. He picked up plenty of pointers while hosting a cooking show with the inimitable Martha Stewart! Martha also has her own wine with 19 Crimes: <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fwhite-wine%2Fchardonnay%2F19-crimes-marthas-chardonnay%2Fp%2F244087750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fwhite-wine%2Fchardonnay%2F19-crimes-marthas-chardonnay%2Fp%2F244087750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Martha&rsquo;s Chard</a>.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Domaine-Ste.-Michelle-Brut_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=892" alt="Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 5"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$14.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fdomaine-ste-michelle-brut%2Fp%2F1487750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut" data-product-price="14.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">14.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>If you prefer a dryer sparkling wine, our team suggests adding&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fdomaine-ste-michelle-brut%2Fp%2F1487750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fdomaine-ste-michelle-brut%2Fp%2F1487750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut</a> to your list of must-try cheap champagnes.</p><p>This wine is made in Washington&rsquo;s Columbia Valley, a climate very similar to Champagne, France. You&rsquo;ll often see this brut labeled as American-style champagne&mdash;and it tastes like one!</p><p>This well-balanced, semi-dry sparkling wine has tart, Granny Smith apple notes, whispers of citrus and a toasty finish. While a bottle of Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut will only cost you about $12, &ldquo;it still feels special,&rdquo; says Catherine.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Chloe-Prosecco_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=892" alt="Chloe Prosecco" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 6"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Chloe Prosecco</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$14.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fprosecco%2Fchloe-prosecco%2Fp%2F159898750" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="Chloe Prosecco" data-product-price="14.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">14.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>For a fizz that stays and a flavor you&rsquo;ll adore, our Test Kitchen suggests <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fprosecco%2Fchloe-prosecco%2Fp%2F159898750" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fprosecco%2Fchloe-prosecco%2Fp%2F159898750" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Chloe Prosecco</a>.</p><p>This affordable sparkling wine is full of bubbles of all sizes. The smaller ones linger to help keep that fizzy feeling even after you&rsquo;ve been holding your glass for a bit.</p><p>Though, with the tart, fruit-forward flavors of this Italian bubbly, our Test Kitchen doesn&rsquo;t anticipate you holding onto your <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-wine-glasses-according-to-experts/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-wine-glasses-according-to-experts/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">stemware</a> for very long. This Prosecco hits all the right notes with a bit of green apple and nice acidity. &ldquo;It&rsquo;s very clean and bright,&rdquo; explains Shannon.&nbsp; &ldquo;I&rsquo;d be happy to toast with this one,&rdquo; she says.</p><hr><video id="T0733MN" title="Test Kitchen Preferred" data-description="Check out this video about our Test Kitchen Preferred process" poster="http://content.jwplatform.com/v2/media/ALzZ8JJI/poster.jpg?width=720" data-portal-copyright="Taste of Home"><source src="http://content.jwplatform.com/videos/ALzZ8JJI-OOHHzDJg.mp4" type="video/mp4"></source></video><h2>We Sampled 20 Bottles Under $20</h2><p>For this test, our <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/meet-the-taste-of-home-test-kitchen-team/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/meet-the-taste-of-home-test-kitchen-team/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Test Kitchen team</a> (many of whom are serious bubbly fanatics) sampled a whopping 20 kinds of affordable champagne in a blind <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/test-kitchen/taste-tests/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/test-kitchen/taste-tests/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">taste test</a>. That&rsquo;s right&mdash;no peeking!</p><p>But a few words on this cheap champagne taste test. To start, sparkling wine can only be called <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-is-champagne/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-is-champagne/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Champagne</a> if it comes from the Champagne region of France. If the wine comes from another region&mdash;even if it&rsquo;s elsewhere in France&mdash;it&rsquo;ll be called by another name. This being said, champagne (with a lower case &lsquo;c&rsquo;) has become the shorthand phrase for sparkling wine.</p><p>So for this test, our team used this expanded definition of champagne. They popped open bottles of all kinds of bubbly like Prosecco (an Italian bubbly), Cava (a Spanish sparkler) and even American sparkling wines. Each brand our team selected was under $20 and was scored for fizz and flavor.</p><h2>FAQ</h2><h3>Where can I buy cheap champagne?</h3><p>You can find cheap champagne at most grocery stores that sell alcohol, but one of our favorite places to order from online is <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2F" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2F" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">TotalWine.com</a>.</p><h3>How much is a cheap bottle of champagne?</h3><p>Cheap bottles of champagne ring up for $5 to $20.</p><h3>Does cheap champagne go bad?</h3><p>Cheap champagne, like other champagnes, go bad eventually. If you open your champagne, you can keep it for no longer than three days in the fridge.</p><div class="listicle-card-image-wrapper"><p data-wp-editing="1"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="size-large wp-image-1783324 aligncenter" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Taste-of-Home-Test_Kitchen-Preferred-The-Best-Products-Chosen-by-Our-Experts.gif?fit=700%2C694" alt="Taste Of Home Test Kitchen Preferred The Best Products Chosen By Our Experts" width="700" height="694" data-image-analytics='{"licensorName":"not available","credits":"Taste of Home"}' data-recalc-dims="1" title="Taste Of Home Test Kitchen Preferred The Best Products Chosen By Our Experts" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Taste of Home"></p></div><h2>Why You Should Trust Us</h2><p>Our Test Kitchen is constantly trying out new food, kitchen gadgets and cleaning gear. We put every product through a thorough&nbsp;<a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/about-product-testing/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/about-product-testing/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">testing process</a>. Then our Test Kitchen team chooses the winners. Those best-tasting and top-performing products get our stamp of approval: to be called <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/test-kitchen-preferred/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/test-kitchen-preferred/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Test Kitchen-Preferred</a>.</p><p>If you want to fill your pantry and fridge with the best products, check out these other tests:</p><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-rose/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-rose/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">The best ros&eacute;</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-light-beer-brands/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-light-beer-brands/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">The best light beer</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-margarita-mix/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-margarita-mix/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">The best margarita mix</a></li></ul><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/the-best-cheap-champagne/">Cheers to the Best Cheap Champagne (Under $20 a Pop!)</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
